msg:Choosing this hotel to go to Gulangyu Island is definitely the right choice. First of all, their unique dock pick-up service is really labor-saving, especially when we are tired of playing on the island, we can walk to the dock and arrange a hotel shuttle to pick you up and take you back to the hotel. Manager Chen in the hotel lobby is very nice. He took the initiative to call me and add WeChat early to ask if I need any help, and arranged everything I can think of in advance. There is also the battery car master Chen, who is very kind and makes guests feel at home. He talked to us a lot of interesting things and precautions on the island on the shuttle bus, and took the initiative to help us move our luggage.
Let's talk about the hotel:
Service: I have stayed in so many five-star hotels, and I feel that their service is even better than others;
Environment: The hotel has a beautiful environment, the outdoor swimming pool is beautiful, there are little squirrels and parrots, the hotel is well-planned, warm and comfortable, the beach and Gulang Stone are opposite the hotel, and the hotel also provides plastic slippers, which is very convenient;
Hygiene: The aunt cleans every day, and the bed sheets and quilt covers are also changed every day, which many five-star hotels cannot do;
Facilities: The facilities are very good and very petty;
Breakfast: The breakfast should be mentioned in particular. This hotel is in the top five of the many hotels I have stayed in. Although there are not many styles, they are all fine products, especially the Shacha noodles, which can be said to be the best I have ever eaten.
If I go to Gulangyu again, I will choose this hotel and recommend it to my friends.

posted:Posted June 4, 2024
msg:The hotel entrance faces one of the Gulang stones on Gulangyu Island, and the balcony of the room I booked (1201) faces this Gulang stone. This room has a good view!
The hotel service is considerate. Manager Chen will contact you in advance to see if you need to be picked up from the pier. If there are any problems later, he can help you solve them in time. This must be praised. The room is clean and hygienic, and the facilities are complete. The TV is a little small, but unexpectedly, it can be projected from a mobile phone. You need to contact the waiter to help you.
There are not too many breakfast varieties, but it can basically meet different needs. Local noodles are also a good choice.
The hotel is close to Neicuoao Pier. It takes more than 20 minutes to walk to Sunlight Rock. The island is actually not big and can be reached on foot. There are just many attractions. It takes special forces to walk through it in one day. It is recommended to play in two days.
About the hotel's special services
Afternoon tea for two: This is a gift, and it is served on the second floor of the restaurant. It is good!
Neicuoao Pier shuttle bus picks up and drops off at the hotel (reservation must be made at least 2 hours in advance): The pick-up and drop-off service is provided, which must be praised, bringing great convenience to travel. But please note that only Neicuoao Pier is provided, so please make sure to check the pier where the ferry ticket arrives.
Overall satisfied, recommended!
